2



                          what
                          we do
                          we enable our customers to turn risks into rewards
                          by helping them to identify assess and manage their
                          most critical risks that includes assisting customers
                          in balancing a wide range of technical operational
                          business and societal aspects to optimize performance

                          in addition we verify or certify compliance with
                          standards rules and regulations in order to safeguard
                          life property and the environment as such we perform
                          a balancing act between business and society
